Use TI= to search in the title, AB= for the abstract, CL= for the claims, or TAC= for all three. For example, TI=(safety belt).

Search by Cooperative Patent Classifications (CPCs): These are commonly used to represent ideas in place of keywords, and can also be entered in a search term box. If you're searching forseat belts, you could also search for B60R22/00 to retrieve documents that mention safety belts or body harnesses. CPC=B60R22 will match documents with exactly this CPC, CPC=B60R22/low matches documents with this CPC or a child classification of this CPC.

Keywords and boolean syntax (USPTO or EPO format): seat belt searches these two words, or their plurals and close synonyms. "seat belt" searches this exact phrase, in order. -seat -belt searches for documents not containing either word.

For searches using boolean logic, the default operator is AND with left associativity. Note: this means safety OR seat belt is searched as (safety OR seat) AND belt. Each word automatically includes plurals and close synonyms. Adjacent words that are implicitly ANDed together, such as (safety belt), are treated as a phrase when generating synonyms.

Compositions and methods for hydroxylating epothilones

Abstract
translated from

Isolated nucleic acid sequences and polypeptides encoded thereby for epothilone B hydroxylase and mutants and variants thereof and a ferredoxin located downstream from the epothilone B hydroxylase gene are provided. Also provided are vectors and cells containing these vectors. In addition, methods for producing recombinant microorganisms, methods for using these recombinant microorganism to produce hydroxyalkyl-bearing epothilones and an epothilone analog produced by a mutant of epothilone B hydroxylase are provided.

Figure 1 presents a diagrammatic illustration of epothilone B turning into Escherichia coli in actinomycete strain SC15847 (ATCC PT-1 0 4 3)-later identified as Amycolatopsis orientalis, described in WO 00/3 92 76 Biotransformation of Talimycin F. -8- (3) (3) 200418849 Cytochrome P-4 50 enzymes are present in prokaryotic and eukaryotic cells and collectively have a ^ heme binding function fn 'This functional site is associated with carbon monoxide After recombination, they can be distinguished by the absorption peak at 450 nm. Cytochrome P-4 50 enzymes can perform a wide range of oxidative reactions with alkanes on predominantly hydrophobic substrates, including aromatic and benzoic rings. In prokaryotes, they exist as a detoxification system and serve as the first enzymatic step to metabolize substrates such as toluene, benzene and camphor. Cytochrome P-450 enzymes are also present in secondary metabolite biosynthetic pathways, such as nikkomycin (Bruntner, C. et al., 1 999, Mol. Gen. Genet. 262) in Streptomyces tendae. 1 02- 1 1 4), doxorubicin (Dickens, ML, Strohl, WR, 1 996, J. Bacteriol, 1 7 8: 3 3 8 9-3 3 9 5) and epothilone Biosynthetic clusters (Julien, B. et al., 2000, Gene, 249: 153-16 0). With few exceptions, the cytochrome P-4 50 system is composed of three proteins in prokaryotes ... one is the iron redox protein NADH or NADH-dependent reductase, the other is iron-thioferredoxin and Cytochrome P-450 enzymes (Lewis, DF, Hlavica, P., 2000, Biochem. Biophys. Acta., 1 460: 3 5 3 -3 74). The electron system is transferred from ferredoxin reductase to ferredoxin and finally to the cytochrome P-450 enzyme to promote the division of molecular oxygen. [Summary of the Invention] An object of the present invention is to propose an isolated nucleic acid sequence encoding epothilone B hydroxylase and a variant or mutant thereof, and encode ferredoxin-9- (4) (4) 200418849 or An isolated nucleic acid sequence of a variant or mutant thereof. Another item of the present invention is to propose an isolated polypeptide comprising an amino acid sequence possessed by epothilone B enzyme and its variants or mutants, and an enzyme comprising ferredoxin and its variants or mutants. Isolated polypeptide of amino acid sequence. Another item of the present invention is to propose the structural coordinates of an epothilone B hydroxylase homogeneity model. The structural coordinates are those listed in Appendix i. This model of the present invention provides a tool for designing modulators of the biological functions of epothilone B hydroxylase and other mutants of epothilone B enzyme with altered specificity. Another item of the present invention is to propose a vector comprising an isolated nucleic acid encoding epothilone B hydroxylase or a variant or mutant thereof and / or a ferredoxin or a variant or mutant thereof. sequence. In a preferred embodiment, these vectors further include a nucleic acid sequence encoding a ferredoxin. Another item of the present invention is to propose a host cell comprising a vector containing a vector encoding epothilone B hydroxylase or a variant or mutant thereof and / or a ferredoxin or a variant or mutant thereof. Nucleic acid sequence. Another item of the present invention is to propose a method for producing recombinant microorganisms. These recombinant microorganisms can hydroxylate compounds having terminal alkyl groups, especially epothilones, to produce compounds having terminal hydroxyalkyl groups. Compounds. Another item of the present invention is to propose a recombinantly produced microorganism capable of hydroxylating a compound having a terminal alkyl group, particularly epothilone-10- (5) (5) 200418849 to produce Terminal hydroxyalkyl compounds. Another item of the present invention is to propose a method for hydroxylating a compound in such a recombinant microorganism. In particular, the present invention proposes a method for producing epothilone loaded with a hydroxyl group. Three highly conserved regions were identified, in the I-helix, containing oxygen-binding functional sites, in the K-helix, and across B-bulge and L-spirals, containing conserved blood matrix-binding functional sites. The genomic fragment is then amplified by polymerase chain reaction (PCR). After PCR amplification, the reaction product was separated by gel electrophoresis and a fragment having a desired size was cut out. DNA was extracted from agarose gel slices using the Qiaquick gel extraction program (Qiagen, Santa Clarita, California, USA). The fragments were then cloned into a PCRscript vector (Stratagene, La Jolla, California, USA) using a PCRscript Amp selection kit (Stratagene). At 30-37 ° C ′ at 230-300 (13) 200418849 r pm, 16-24 hours, the colonies containing the inserts were picked up in ml of LB liquid medium containing 100 μg / ml of ampicillin. Use this plastid DNA as a PCR and sequencing template and for restriction digestion analysis.

A "variant", as used in the present invention, is intended to include its amino acid sequence with conservative amino acid substitutions relative to SEQ ID NO: 2 or 4, and it has been shown to exhibit similarity to SEQ ID NO: 2 Or 4 biologically active or functional polypeptide. "Conservative amino acid substitution" is intended to include aliphatic amino acids such as between Ala, Val, Leu and lie, between hydroxyl residues Ser and Thr, between acidic residues Asp and Glu, and amidine residues Asn Permutation with Gin. Exemplary amino acid sequences of the variants of the present invention are shown in SEQ ID NO: 4 3-4 9 and the amino acid substitutions of these exemplary variants are listed in Table 2 above. The term "mutant" as used herein is intended to include a nucleic acid sequence encoded by one or more point mutations, or deletions or additions of a nucleic acid, but still similar, as compared to SEQ ID NO: 1 or 3 A polypeptide having activity in the polypeptide encoded by SEQ ID NO: 1 or 3. In a preferred embodiment, a mutation in a nucleic acid is one that alters the specificity and / or yield of the polypeptide encoded by it. Proteins 23, 4 0 3 - 1 4, 1 99 5 ) 等的一般敘述於已知的同源蛋白質EryF (PDB Code 1 KIN 鏈A)所具構造之基礎上構造出埃坡黴素B羥化酶的立體 模型。此等序列之間的同質率爲3 4%。圖3繪示出埃坡黴 素B羥化酶序列（SEQ ID NO:2)與EryF序列（PDB Code 1KIN鏈 A ; SEQ ID NO:76)的排比。圖4繪示出根據與 EryF的序列排比所得埃坡黴素B羥化酶的同質模型。 -32- (27) (27)200418849 此外也製備出相對於EryF (PDB Code 1KIN)的埃坡徽 素B羥化酶之能量標繪圖且示於圖5之中。使用在一所給 殘基位置的5 1個殘基之平均窗尺寸來計算以該所給殘基 爲中心位置的序列中所含該5 1個殘基的能量平均値。如 圖5中所示者，沿著序列的所有能量都低於0，因而顯不 如圖4和附錄1所揭示的模型構造係合理者。 在圖4埃坡黴素B羥化酶同質模型中所表的立體構造 係由在附錄1中所列出的一組構造座標所界定者。”構造 座標”一術語指的是從該同質模型的構建中產生的笛卡爾 座標（Cartesian coordinates)。不過，如諸於此技者所了解 者，對於一蛋白質的一組構造座標爲界定在三次元內的形 狀之一相對點組。因此，一完全不同的座標組可能界定一 類似或相同的形狀。再者，個別座標的輕微變異，如在產 生同質模型中使用不同的排比模板及/或使用不同的方法 產生類似的同質模型所發生者，對於整體形狀都會有小幅 影響。座標的變異也會因爲構造座標的數學演算而產生。 例如，附錄1中所列出的構造座標可經由構造座標的分數 化（fractionalization)來演算；對構造座標組的整數的加或 減，構造座標的反演（inversion)或上述的任何組合。 所以需要各種計算分析來決定一分子或其部份相對於 上文所述埃坡黴素B羥化酶的全部或部份足夠相似到可視 爲相同之程度。此等分析都可以在現行的軟體應用中進 行，例如 SYBYL 第 6.7 版或 INSIGHTII(Molecular Simulations Inc., San Diego，CA)第 2000 版以及如在所附 (28) (28)200418849 的使用者指引中所述者。 舉例而言，在程式SYBYL中的重疊工具可用來在不 同的構造之間及在相同構造的不同構象（conformation)之 間進行比較。於S YB YL中比較構造所用的程序係分爲四 個步驟：1 )裝載所要比較的構造；2)在此等構造中界定 原子等價（equivalency) ; 3)實施擬合運算；及4)分析 結果。每一構造都由一名稱所鑑別。一構造經鑑別爲標的 (亦即，固定構造）；第二構造（亦即，移動構造）經鑑別爲 # 來源構造。由於SYBYL內的原子等價係由使用者輸入所 界定，爲了本發明此方面的目的，乃將等價原子定義爲對 於要比較的兩種構造之間的所有保守性殘基所含的蛋白質 骨架原子（N、C a、C和0)。另外，只有考慮剛性擬合運 算。於使用剛性擬合方法之時，將所操作的構造平移和旋 轉以得到與標的構造之最佳擬合。該擬合運算係使用可計 算出要施用於移動構造的最佳平移和旋轉之算法，使得對 所指定的等價原子對所得擬合値之均方根差値爲一絕對最 I 低値。此値隨即由SYBYL以埃（Α)爲單位報告出。 爲本發明目的而言，任何埃坡黴素B羥化酶同質模型 在重疊於附錄1中所列構造座標所述的對應骨架原子時， 其保守性殘基骨架原子（N、C a、C、0)所具均方根差値 小於約4.0 Α者皆視爲是相同者。更佳者，該均方根差値 爲小於約3.0 The three-dimensional structure shown in Fig. 4 epothilone B hydroxylase homogeneity model is defined by a set of structural coordinates listed in Appendix 1. The term "structural coordinates" refers to Cartesian coordinates derived from the construction of the homogeneous model. However, as known to those skilled in the art, a set of structural coordinates for a protein is a set of relative points of a shape defined within a three-dimensional shape. Therefore, a completely different set of coordinates may define a similar or identical shape. Furthermore, slight variations in individual coordinates, such as those using different alignment templates and / or different methods to generate similar homogeneous models in the generation of homogeneous models, will have a small impact on the overall shape. Variations in coordinates are also caused by mathematical calculations that construct the coordinates. For example, the structural coordinates listed in Appendix 1 may be calculated via fractionalization of the structural coordinates; addition or subtraction of integers from the structural coordinate group, inversion of the structural coordinates, or any combination thereof. Therefore, various computational analyses are required to determine whether a molecule or a part thereof is sufficiently similar to all or a part of the epothilone B hydroxylase described above to be regarded as the same degree. These analyses can be performed in existing software applications, such as SYBYL version 6.7 or INSIGHTII (Molecular Simulations Inc., San Diego, CA) version 2000 and user guides as attached (28) (28) 200418849 As described. For example, the overlap tool in the program SYBYL can be used to compare between different configurations and between different conformations of the same configuration. The procedure for comparing structures in S YB YL is divided into four steps: 1) loading the structures to be compared; 2) defining atomic equivalence in these structures; 3) performing a fitting operation; and 4) Analyze the results. Each construct is identified by a name. One structure was identified as the target (i.e., a fixed structure); the second structure (i.e., a mobile structure) was identified as the #source structure. Since the atomic equivalence in SYBYL is defined by user input, for the purposes of this aspect of the invention, equivalent atoms are defined as the protein backbone contained in all conservative residues between the two constructs to be compared Atoms (N, Ca, C, and 0). In addition, only rigid fit calculations are considered. When using the rigid fitting method, the operated structure is translated and rotated to obtain the best fit with the target structure. This fitting operation uses an algorithm that can calculate the best translation and rotation to be applied to the moving structure, so that the root mean square difference 値 of the fitted 对 for the specified equivalent atom pair is an absolute minimum 値. This case was reported by SYBYL in units of Angstrom (Α). For the purposes of the present invention, when any homogenous model of epothilone B hydroxylase overlaps with the corresponding backbone atom described in the structural coordinates listed in Appendix 1, its conservative residue backbone atom (N, C a, C , 0) Those with a root mean square difference 値 less than about 4.0 A are considered to be the same. More preferably, the root mean square difference 値 is less than about 3.0 A. More preferably, the root mean square difference is less than about 2.0 A. For the purposes of the present invention, any epothilone B hydroxylase homogeneous model-34- (29) (29) 200418849 overlaps with the corresponding backbone atom described in the structural coordinates listed in Appendix 1, its conservative residues The base skeleton atoms (N, C a, C, 〇) have root mean square differences 値 less than about 2.0 A are considered to be the same. More preferably, the root mean square difference 値 is less than about 1. ο A. In another specific example of the present invention, when the structural model in which the skeleton atom is replaced by other elements overlaps with the corresponding skeleton atom, those having a low root mean square difference are considered to be the same. For example, the homogeneous model of its original skeleton carbon and / or nitrogen and / or oxygen atoms replaced with other elements has approximately 4.0 A when overlapping with the corresponding skeleton atoms described in the structural coordinates listed in Appendix 1. The better is about 3.0 A, and even the better is about 2 A. The root mean square difference is considered to be the same. The term "root-mean-square difference" means the square root of the arithmetic mean 平方 of the square of the deviation 値 from the mean 値. It is a way of expressing deviations or variations from a trend or a goal. For the purpose of the present invention, "root mean square difference" refers to the definition of the relevant part of a protein backbone relative to the backbone of the epothilone B hydroxylase moiety contained in the complex defined by the structural coordinates described herein. The design within these modeled systems is usually based on compounds capable of physically and structurally associating with epothilone B chemical enzymes. In addition to this -38-(33) (33) 200418849, the compound must be able to work out a conformation that allows it to associate with epothilone B hydroxylase. These modeled systems can estimate the potential inhibitory or binding effects of a potential epothilone B hydroxylase substrate or modulator before actual synthesis and testing. Methods for screening chemicals or fragments for their ability to associate with a given protein target are also well known. These methods often start without visually checking the joints on a computer screen. The selected fragment or chemical is then placed in the binding region of epothilone B hydroxylase. Docking is done using software such as INSIGHTII, QUANTA and SYBYL, followed by energy minimization and molecular dynamics using standard molecular mechanical force fields such as MMFF, CHARMM and AMBER. Examples of computer programs that are useful in the selection of chemical fragments or chemical bodies that can be used in the present invention include, but are not limited to, GRID (Goodford, 1 9 8 5), AUTODOCK (Goodsell, 1 990), and DOCK (Kuntz et al., 1 9 82) ° After selecting the better chemistries or fragments, they can be visually checked for their relationship with epothilone B hydroxylase and then assembled into a single potential modulator. Therefore, another aspect of the present invention relates to a recombinantly produced microorganism that can express epothilone B hydroxylase alone or together with ferredoxin and that the microorganism is capable of converting a compound having a terminal alkyl group, particularly It is epothilone, which is hydroxylated and made into a terminal hydroxyalkyl group. The recombinantly produced microbial silicon is produced by transforming a cell such as a bacterial cell using a plastid including a nucleic acid sequence encoding an epothilone B hydroxylase. In a preferred embodiment, the cell lines use a nucleic acid sequence comprising an epothilone B ® ase or a mutant or variant thereof, and a cell line located downstream of the epothilone B hydroxylase gene. The plastids of the nucleic acid sequence encoding the ferredoxin are transformed. Examples of microorganisms that can be transformed using these plastids to produce the recombinant microorganism of the present invention include, but are not limited to, E. coli, Bacillus megaterium, Streptomyces orientalis, -43- (38) (38) 200418849 Sorangiumce 11 u 1 osum, Rhodococcus erythropolis, and streptomyces species such as Streptomyces lividans, Streptomyces virginiae, Streptomyces venezuelae , Streptomyces a 1 bus, Streptomyces coelicolor, Streptomyces griseus and Streptomyces griseus o The recombinantly produced microorganisms of the present invention can be used in microbial programs or methods to produce Compounds with terminal hydroxyalkyl groups, and especially epothilones. Generally, a recombinantly-produced microorganism or a microorganism capable of selectively hydroxylating a terminal carbon or an alkyl group can be cultured in an aqueous nutrient medium containing assimilable carbon and nitrogen sources in the presence of an appropriate substrate under submerged aerobic conditions, or The enzymes derived from it produce hydroxyalkyl-loaded products. Suitable epothilones used as substrates in the method of the present invention may be any of these compounds having a terminal carbon or alkyl group capable of accepting the enzymatic hydroxylation of the present invention. The starting materials, or substrates, can be isolated from natural sources, such as P. cellulosae, or they can be synthetically formed epothilones. Any other substrate capable of accepting enzymatic hydroxylation with a terminal carbon or alkyl group can also be used in the method of the present invention. For example, compactin can be used as a substrate, which after hydroxylation will form the compound pravastatin. A typical growth medium includes the required carbon source, nitrogen source, and trace elements. You can also add -46- (41) 200418849 to the inducer in the medium. "Inducer," as used herein, includes any compound that enhances the formation of a desired enzyme activity in recombinantly produced cells. Typical inducers used in the present invention may include solvents used to dissolve substrates, such as dimethylamine Sodium, dimethylformamide, dioxane, ethanol, and acetone. In addition, certain substrates, such as epothilone B, can also be considered as inducers.

碳源可包括糖類例如葡萄糖、果糖、半乳糖、麥芽 糖、蔗糖、甘露糖、山梨糖、甘油、澱粉和類似者；有機 酸例如乙酸鈉、棒檬酸鈉、和類似者；及醇類例如乙醇、 丙醇和類似者。較佳的碳源包括，但不限於、葡萄糖、果 糖、蔗糖、甘油和澱粉。 氮源可包括N-Z胺A、玉米浸液、大豆粉、牛肉萃取 物、胰蛋白腺（tryptone)、胃蛋白腺（peptone)、棉子粉、 花生粉、胺基酸例如榖胺酸鈉和類似者，檸檬酸鈉、硫酸 銨和類似者。Carbon sources may include sugars such as glucose, fructose, galactose, maltose, sucrose, mannose, sorbose, glycerol, starch, and the like; organic acids such as sodium acetate, sodium limonate, and the like; and alcohols such as ethanol , Propanol and the like. produce microtubule-stabilizing agents and new compounds that are expected to be useful as microtubule-stabilizing agents, including Ipo Mycin analogs such as 24-hydroxy-epothilone B (formula A) and pharmaceutically acceptable salts thereof. Microtubule stabilizers made using these compositions and methods can be used to treat a variety of cancers and other proliferative diseases including, but not limited to, the following: Cancer, including bladder, breast, colon, kidney, liver, lung , Ovary, pancreas, stomach, cervix, thyroid and skin; including squamous cell carcinoma; lymphoid hematopoietic tumors, including leukemia, acute lymphocytic leukemia, acute lymphoblastic leukemia, B-cell lymphoma , T-cell lymphoma, 〇dgkins lymphoma, non-Ηdgkins lymphoma, hair cell lymphoma, and Burketts lymphoma; tumors of mesenchymal origin, including fibrosarcoma and rhabdomyosarcoma, and other tumors, including melanoma, seminoma Semioma, Teratocarcinoma, neuroblastoma and glioma; tumors of the central and peripheral nervous system, including astrocytoma, neuroblastoma, glioma, and Schwannomas (schwa η η 〇mas); mesenchymal tumors 'including fibrosarcoma, rhabdomyosarcoma and osteosarcoma; and other tumors' including melanoma , Xen〇derma pigmentosum, kefatoactanthoma, seminoma, thyroid follicular carcinoma and teratoma. The microtubule stabilizer prepared by using the composition and method of the present invention can also inhibit angiogenesis, thereby affecting tumor growth and providing treatment for tumors and tumor-related disorders. These anti-angiogenic -55- (50) 200418849 properties of these compounds can also be used to treat other conditions that are responsive to anti-angiogenic agents including, but not limited to, a blood blindness associated with retinal angiogenesis, Arthritis, especially inflammatory arthritis, multiple sclerosis, retinitis and psoriasis. The microtubule stabilizer prepared by using the composition and method of the present invention can induce or inhibit apoptosis, a physiological cell death process that is critical for normal development and homeostasis. Changes in the apoptotic pathway can contribute to the pathogenesis of many human diseases. The compounds of the present invention, such as those shown in I and 11 and Formula A, can be used to treat a variety of human diseases with apoptotic abnormalities when used as modulators of apoptosis, including, but not limited to, cancer and precancerous Lesions, immune response-related diseases, viral infections, degenerative diseases of the musculoskeletal system and kidney disease. Without wishing to be bound by any mechanism or morphology, microtubule stabilizers made using the compositions and methods of the invention can also be used to treat conditions other than cancer or other proliferative diseases. These conditions include, but are not limited to, viral infections such as herpes virus, scar virus, Epstein-Barr virus, Sindbis virus, and adenovirus; autoimmune diseases such as systemic lupus erythematosus, immune-mediated glomerulonephritis, rheumatic joints Inflammation, psoriasis, inflammatory bowel disease and autoimmune diabetes; neurodegenerative diseases such as Alzheimer's disease, AIDS-related dementia, Parkinson's disease, amyotrophic lateral sclerosis, pigmented retinitis, Spinal muscular atrophy and cerebellar degeneration; AIDS; Symptoms of Spinal Cord Dysplasia; Aplastic Anemia; Hemostatic Injury Associated with Myocardial Infarction; Stroke and Reinfusion Injury; Narrow SSS; Narrow Rhythm; Atherosclerosis Toxin-induced or alcohol-induced liver disease -56- (51) (51) 200418849 disease; hematological diseases such as chronic anemia and aplastic anemia; degenerative diseases of the musculoskeletal system such as osteoporosis and arthritis; aspirin- Sensitive sinusitis; cystic fibrosis; multiple sclerosis; kidney disease; and cancer pain. 使用胍-淸潔劑溶胞法，DNAzol劑（Invitrogen, Carlsbad, California，USA)從東方鏈黴菌土壤離析菌株編 號 SC 1 5 8 47 (ATCC PT- 1 043 )者分離出基因組 DNA。將 SC 1 5 847培養物再28°C的F7培養基（葡萄糖2.2%、酵母 菌萃取物1.0%、麥芽萃取物1.0%，胃蛋白腺0.1%、pH 7 . 〇 )中生長2 4小時。經由離心收取2 0毫升培養物並再懸 浮於 20毫升 DNAzol內，經由抽吸予以混合且在 Backman TJ6離心機中離心10分鐘。加入10毫升100% 乙醇，倒轉數次，並存放於室溫下3分鐘。將DNA捲繞 於一玻璃吸量管上，在1 〇〇%乙醇內洗滌並使其空氣乾燥 1〇分鐘。將沉九再懸浮於5 00微升8 mM NaOH內且於溶 解後，使用30微升1 M HEP ES pH 7.2予以中和。 -60- (55) 200418849 實施例3 : PCR反應Genomic DNA was isolated from a Streptomyces orientalis soil isolate strain number SC 1 5 8 47 (ATCC PT-1 043) using a guanidine-detergent lysis method and DNAzol agent (Invitrogen, Carlsbad, California, USA). The SC 1 5 847 culture was grown in F7 medium (glucose 2.2%, yeast extract 1.0%, malt extract 1.0%, gastric protein gland 0.1%, pH 7.0) at 28 ° C for 24 hours. 20 ml of the culture was collected by centrifugation and resuspended in 20 ml of DNAzol, mixed by suction and centrifuged in a Backman TJ6 centrifuge for 10 minutes. Add 10 ml of 100% ethanol, invert several times, and store at room temperature for 3 minutes. The DNA was wound on a glass pipette, washed in 100% ethanol and allowed to air dry for 10 minutes. Shen Jiu was resuspended in 500 microliters of 8 mM NaOH and after dissolution, it was neutralized with 30 microliters of 1 M HEP ES pH 7.2. -60- (55) 200418849 Example 3: PCR reaction

Spectra were collected using a scan range of m / z 100 to 600 at an acquisition rate of 10 MS / sec. The ionization technology used is cationic electrospray (ES). Example 17: Mutation Generation of the ebh Gene to Improve Yield or Change Specificity Using the Quikchange® XL Site-Directed Mutagenesis Kit and Quikchange® Multi Site-Directed Mutagenesis Kit from Stratagene to introduce mutations in the coding region of the ebh gene . Both methods use a 35-45 base DNA primer containing the desired mutation (SEQ ID NO: 5 4-5 9 fP 77), a methylated circular plastid template, and PfuTUr * b〇® DNA polymerase (U.S. Patent Nos. 5,545,552 and 5,866,395 and 5,948,663) to produce a copy of a plastid template with mutations contained in mutation-generating primers. The reactant was subsequently digested with the endonuclease enzyme Dpnl to selectively digest the methylated plastid template, but left intact unmethylated mutant plastids. All procedures were followed by the manufacturer's instructions, except that the incubation time was increased from 1 hour to 3 hours during the Dpnl digestion step. The pPCRscript-ebh vector was used as a template for mutation generation. Transform 1 to 2 microliters of the reaction into XL 1-Blue® electric competent cells or XL10-Gold® super competent cells (SUatagene). Biotransformation products It was dissolved at about 7.5 minutes and the flow was manually stopped to keep the lysate in the NMR probe for NMR data collection. Isolation and analysis were performed as follows. The butanol / methanol extraction solution (about 10%) was used. Ml) was evaporated to dryness under a stream of nitrogen. To the residue (38 mg) was added 1 ml of methanol and the insoluble matter was removed by centrifugation (13 000 r * pm, 2 minutes). 0.1 ml of the upper solution was used LC / NMR studies and preparative HPLC with the remaining 0.9 mL (0.2-0.4 mL per injection). Two main chromatographic peaks were observed and collected Peak A was eluted between 14 and 15 minutes, and Peak B was eluted between 1 6.5 and 1 7.5 minutes. Analytical HPLC analysis revealed the peak B micro-mother compound, epothilone B (Rt 8.5 minutes) and peak A is a biotransformation product (Rt 7.3 minutes). Peak A liquid was combined and MS analysis data was obtained with the combined liquid. The combined liquid was evaporated to a small volume, and then freeze-dried. 3 mg of white solid was obtained. NMR and HPLC analysis of the white solid (dissolved in methanol) revealed that the biotransformation product was partially decomposed during the drying process. [Schematic description]
